the barrier event, the option becomes worthless,\n49:  * or alternatively, a rebate is made.\n50:  */\n51: @BeanDefinition\n52: public final class FxSingleBarrierOption\n53:     implements FxOptionProduct, Resolvable<ResolvedFxSingleBarrierOption>, ImmutableBean, Serializable {\n54: \n55:   /**\n56:    * The underlying FX vanilla option.\n57:    */\n58:   @PropertyDefinition(validate = \"notNull\")\n59:   private final FxVanillaOption underlyingOption;\n60:   /**\n61:    * The barrier description.\n62:    * <p>\n63:    * The barrier level stored in this field must be represented based on the direction of the currency pair in the\n64:    * underlying FX transaction.\n65:    * <p>\n66:    * For example, if the underlying option is an option on EUR/GBP, the barrier should be a certain level of EUR/GBP rate.\n67:    */\n68:   @PropertyDefinition(validate = \"notNull\")\n69:   private final Barrier barrier;\n70:   /**\n71:    * For a 'out' option, the amount is paid when the pair.\n75:    * The amount should be positive.\n76:    */\n77:   @PropertyDefinition(get = \"optional\")\n78:   private final CurrencyAmount rebate;\n79: \n80:   //-------------------------------------------------------------------------\n81:   /**\n82:    * Obtains FX single barrier option with rebate.\n83:    *\n84:    * @param underlyingOption  the underlying FX vanilla option\n85:    * @param barrier  the barrier\n86:    * @param rebate  the rebate\n87:    * @return the instance\n88:    */\n89:   public static FxSingleBarrierOption
